         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            I have a multi-project (~10 modules) of which building takes about 20-30 seconds each time. When I press Run in Android Studio, I have to wait every time to rebuild the app, which is extremely slow.
           </p>
           <p>
            Is it possible to automate building process in Android Studio? Or do you have any advice on how to make this process faster?
           </p>
           <p>
            In Eclipse, thanks to automatic building, running the same project on an emulator takes about 3-5 seconds.
           </p>
           <p>
            This is my build.gradle file (app module):
           </p>
           <pre><code>buildscript {
    repositories {
        maven { url 'http://repo1.maven.org/maven2' }
    }
    dependencies {
        classpath 'com.android.tools.build:gradle:0.4'
    }
}
apply plugin: 'android'

dependencies {
    compile fileTree(dir: 'libs', include: '*.jar')
    compile project(':libraries:SharedLibs')
    compile project(':libraries:actionbarsherlock')
    compile project(':libraries:FacebookSDK')
    compile project(':libraries:GooglePlayServices')
    compile project(':libraries:HorizontalGridView')
    compile project(':libraries:ImageViewTouch')
    compile project(':libraries:SlidingMenu')
}

android {
    compileSdkVersion 17
    buildToolsVersion "17.0.0"

    defaultConfig {
        minSdkVersion 8
        targetSdkVersion 16
    }
}
</code></pre>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="19500539">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h2>
             Hardware
            </h2>
            <p>
             I'm sorry, but upgrading development station to SSD and tons of ram has probably a bigger influence than points below combined.
            </p>
            <h2>
             Tools versions
            </h2>
            <p>
             Increasing build performance has major priority for the development teams, so make sure you are using latest
             <a href="https://docs.gradle.org/current/release-notes" rel="noreferrer">
              Gradle
             </a>
             and
             <a href="http://tools.android.com/tech-docs/new-build-system" rel="noreferrer">
              Android Gradle Plugin
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <h2>
             Configuration File
            </h2>
            <p>
             Create a file named
             <code>
              gradle.properties
             </code>
             in whatever directory applies:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               /home/&lt;username&gt;/.gradle/
              </code>
              (Linux)
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               /Users/&lt;username&gt;/.gradle/
              </code>
              (Mac)
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               C:\Users\&lt;username&gt;\.gradle
              </code>
              (Windows)
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Append:
            </p>
            <pre><code># IDE (e.g. Android Studio) users:
# Settings specified in this file will override any Gradle settings
# configured through the IDE.

# For more details on how to configure your build environment visit
# http://www.gradle.org/docs/current/userguide/build_environment.html

# The Gradle daemon aims to improve the startup and execution time of Gradle.
# When set to true the Gradle daemon is to run the build.
# TODO: disable daemon on CI, since builds should be clean and reliable on servers
org.gradle.daemon=true

# Specifies the JVM arguments used for the daemon process.
# The setting is particularly useful for tweaking memory settings.
# https://medium.com/google-developers/faster-android-studio-builds-with-dex-in-process-5988ed8aa37e#.krd1mm27v
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx5120m -XX:MaxPermSize=512m -XX:+HeapDumpOnOutOfMemoryError -Dfile.encoding=UTF-8

# When configured, Gradle will run in incubating parallel mode.
# This option should only be used with decoupled projects. More details, visit
# http://www.gradle.org/docs/current/userguide/multi_project_builds.html#sec:decoupled_projects
org.gradle.parallel=true

# Enables new incubating mode that makes Gradle selective when configuring projects. 
# Only relevant projects are configured which results in faster builds for large multi-projects.
# http://www.gradle.org/docs/current/userguide/multi_project_builds.html#sec:configuration_on_demand
org.gradle.configureondemand=true

# Set to true or false to enable or disable the build cache. 
# If this parameter is not set, the build cache is disabled by default.
# http://tools.android.com/tech-docs/build-cache
android.enableBuildCache=true
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Gradle properties works local if you place them at
             <code>
              projectRoot\gradle.properties
             </code>
             and globally if you place them at
             <code>
              user_home\.gradle\gradle.properties
             </code>
             . Properties applied if you run gradle tasks from console or directly from idea:
            </p>
            <h2>
             IDE Settings
            </h2>
            <p>
             It is possible to tweak Gradle-IntelliJ integration from the IDE settings GUI. Enabling "offline work" (check answer from
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/23648341/624706">
              yava
             </a>
             below) will disable real network requests on every "sync gradle file".
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="IDE settings" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/hGnDg.png"/>
            </p>
            <h2>
             Native multi-dex
            </h2>
            <p>
             One of the slowest steps of the apk build is converting java bytecode into single dex file. Enabling native multidex (minSdk 21 for debug builds only) will help the tooling to reduce an amount of work (check answer from
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/30070657/624706">
              Aksel Willgert
             </a>
             below).
            </p>
            <h2>
             Dependencies
            </h2>
            <p>
             Prefer
             <code>
              @aar
             </code>
             dependencies over library sub-projects.
            </p>
            <p>
             Search aar package on
             <a href="http://search.maven.org/" rel="noreferrer">
              mavenCentral
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="https://bintray.com/bintray/jcenter" rel="noreferrer">
              jCenter
             </a>
             or use
             <a href="https://jitpack.io/" rel="noreferrer">
              jitpack.io
             </a>
             to build any library from github. If you are not editing sources of the dependency library you should not build it every time with your project sources.
            </p>
            <h2>
             Antivirus
            </h2>
            <p>
             Consider to exclude project and cache files from antivirus scanning. This is obviously a trade off with security (don't try this at home!). But if you switch between branches a lot, then antivirus will rescan files before allowing gradle process to use it, which slows build time (in particular AndroidStudio sync project with gradle files and indexing tasks). Measure build time and process CPU with and without antivirus enabled to see if it is related.
            </p>
            <h2>
             Profiling a build
            </h2>
            <p>
             Gradle has built-in support for
             <a href="https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/tutorial_gradle_command_line.html#sec:profiling_build" rel="noreferrer">
              profiling projects
             </a>
             . Different projects are using a different combination of plugins and custom scripts. Using
             <code>
              --profile
             </code>
             will help to find bottlenecks.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2013-10-21T17:02:54" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">
              <div class="js-post-menu pt2" data-post-id="19500539">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Imaging, you have added library like this one:
                 <a href="https://github.com/novak/numberpicker" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  github.com/novak/numberpicker
                 </a>
                 . It has value, providing code solution  for a problem, but author doesn't published it anywhere like maven or jCenter. Now you are either bring that library as sources into your project and build it everytime main project builds or compile it onetime and commit only @aar into your project repository. So it is really a source/binary dependency choice. If you are not editing source you should bring your dependency as precompiled binary. For plain java libraries that is .jar, for android libraries that is .aar
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="23648341">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can ignore gradle update-to-date checks.
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/wrwgo.png"/>
            </p>
            <p>
             For Windows running Android Studio 1.5: Go to
             <code>
              File -&gt; Settings -&gt; Build, Execution, Deployment -&gt; Build tools -&gt; Gradle -&gt; Check Offline work (as shown in image)
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             down from ~30+ sec to ~3 sec
            </p>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="43475746" data-comment-owner-id="423171" data-comment-score="27" id="comment-43475746">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @JohnBallinger Offline work - use this check box to work with Gradle in the offline mode. In this case Gradle will use dependencies from the cache. Gradle will not attempt to access the network to perform dependency resolution. If required dependencies are not present in the dependencies' cache, a build execution will fail. (Source:
                 <a href="http://www.jetbrains.com/idea/help/gradle-2.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  jetbrains.com/idea/help/gradle-2.html
                 </a>
                 )
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Searched everywhere for this and finally found a solution that works for us. Enabling parallel builds (On OSX:
             <code>
              preferences -&gt; compiler -&gt; gradle -&gt; "Compile independent modules in parallel"
             </code>
             ) and enabling 'make project automatically' brought it down from ~1 min to ~20 sec. Thanks to /u/Covalence.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.reddit.com/r/androiddev/comments/1k3nb3/gradle_and_android_studio_way_slower_to_build/" rel="noreferrer">
              http://www.reddit.com/r/androiddev/comments/1k3nb3/gradle_and_android_studio_way_slower_to_build/
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="22598192">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             25
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/22598192/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I recently bought a new SSD and went from Windows to Linux.My build times are now an order of magnitude faster, and no longer annoying.
            </p>
            <p>
             Though it does not directly answer your question as to why it's slower than eclipse, it shows that the process is disk-bounded and an upgrade to an SSD might be a (somewhat expensive) solution. I'm guessing there will be people googling the issue and ending up here, who might appreciate my experience.
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Speed Up Gradle Build In Android Studio 3.2.1
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Ever feel like you are waiting for the builds to complete in Android Studio for minutes? Me too. And it’s a pretty annoying.
Fortunately, there are a few ways that you can use to improve this. Android uses Gradle for building. The latest version is 4.6 has a huge performance boost over previous versions (see Release notes for details).
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 1:
             </strong>
             Update Gradle version
An easier way to accomplish this is to go to: Open Module Settings (your project) &gt; Project Structure
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/xFm0I.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/xFm0I.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              UPDATE
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Change to
             <strong>
              Gradle version: 4.6
             </strong>
             and
Change to
             <strong>
              Android Plugin Version: 3.2.1
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/2hNtg.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/2hNtg.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Download Gradle Release distributive from
             <a href="https://services.gradle.org/distributions/gradle-2.10-all.zip" rel="noreferrer">
              https://services.gradle.org/distributions/gradle-4.6-all.zip
             </a>
             And copy it to the Gradle folder:
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/DNm1e.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/DNm1e.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Last step is to add your discribution in Settings &gt; Gradle
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/jOrQL.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/jOrQL.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Don’t forget to click Apply to save changes.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 2:
             </strong>
             Enable Offline mode, Gradle daemon and parallel build for the project
Offline mode tells Gradle to ignore update-to-date checks. Gradle asks for dependencies everytime and having this option makes it just uses what is already on the machine for dependencies.
Go to Gradle from android studio Setting and click in Offline work box.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/2HeBg.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/2HeBg.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <ol start="2">
             <li>
              Go to Compiler from android studio Setting and add “— offline” in command-line box and click Compile independent modules in parallel.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/W9cgJ.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/W9cgJ.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             The next step is to enable the Gradle daemon and parallel build for your project. Parallel builds will cause your projects with multiple modules (multi-project builds in Gradle) to be built in parallel, which should make large or modular projects build faster.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/Vhps7.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/Vhps7.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             These settings could enabled by modifiing a file named gradle.properties in Gradle scripts directory(i.e., ~/.gradle/gradle.properties).Some of these options (e.g. Complie modules in parallel) are available from Android Studio and also enabled there by default, but putting them in the gradle.properties file will enabled them when building from the terminal and also making sure that your colleagues will use the same settings. But if you’re working on a team, sometimes you can’t commit this stuff.
            </p>
            <pre><code># When configured, Gradle will run in incubating parallel mode.
# This option should only be used with decoupled projects. More details, visit org.gradle.parallel=true
# When set to true the Gradle daemon is used to run the build. For local developer builds this is our favorite property.
# The developer environment is optimized for speed and feedback so we nearly always run Gradle jobs with the daemon.
 org.gradle.daemon=true
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Using the daemon will make your builds startup faster as it won’t have to start up the entire Gradle application every time. The Gradle Daemon is not enabled by default, but it’s recommend always enabling it for developers’ machines (but leaving it disabled for continuous integration servers). FAQ about this mode could be found here
             <a href="https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/gradle_daemon.html" rel="noreferrer">
              https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/gradle_daemon.html
             </a>
             .
The parallel builds setting could be unsafe for some projects. The requirement is that all your modules must be decoupled or your build could fail (see
             <a href="http://gradle.org/docs/current/userguide/multi_project_builds.html#sec:decoupled_projects" rel="noreferrer">
              http://gradle.org/docs/current/userguide/multi_project_builds.html#sec:decoupled_projects
             </a>
             for details).
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 3:
             </strong>
             Enable incremental dexign and tweak memory settings
You can speed up your builds by turning on incremental dexing. In your module’s build file:
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eWQwO.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eWQwO.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Add this option to your android block:
            </p>
            <pre><code>dexOptions {
    incremental true
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             In that dexOptions block you can also specify the heap size for the dex process, for example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>dexOptions {
    incremental true
    javaMaxHeapSize "12g"
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Where “12g” is 12GB of memory. Additional information about this could be found here google.github.io/android-gradle-dsl/current/
You can also configure Gradle parameters in the settings file, e.g. increase the max heap size in case you have a large project:
            </p>
            <pre><code># Specifies the JVM arguments used for the daemon process.
# The setting is particularly useful for tweaking memory settings.
# Default value: -Xmx10248m -XX:MaxPermSize=256m
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx2048m -XX:MaxPermSize=512m -XX:+HeapDumpOnOutOfMemoryError -Dfile.encoding=UTF-8
</code></pre>
            <p>
             See all list of parameters here:
             <a href="https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/userguide_single.html#sec:gradle_configuration_properties" rel="noreferrer">
              https://docs.gradle.org/current/userguide/userguide_single.html#sec:gradle_configuration_properties
             </a>
             for details.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 4:
             </strong>
             Disable Antivirus
Consider to exclude project and cache files from antivirus scanning. This is obviously a trade off with security. But if you switch between branches a lot, then antivirus will rescan files before allowing gradle process to use it, which slows build time (in particular Android Studio sync project with gradle files and indexing tasks). Measure build time and process CPU with and without antivirus enabled to see if it is related.
I hope this helps. Leave a comment if you have any question or some other tips for improving the build performance.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://medium.com/@101/speed-up-gradle-build-in-android-studio-80a5f74ac9ed#.vm894p5iz" rel="noreferrer">
              helpful link
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="30070657" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16775197" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="19" id="answer-30070657" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="30070657">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="19" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             19
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/30070657/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If using google play services, depending on just the libraries you need instead of the whole blob can make things faster.
            </p>
            <p>
             If your only need is maps, use:
            </p>
            <pre><code>compile 'com.google.android.gms:play-services-maps:6.5.+'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             instead of:
            </p>
            <pre><code>compile 'com.google.android.gms:play-services:6.5.+'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The latter brings 20k methods
             <a href="http://jakewharton.com/play-services-is-a-monolith/">
              (see blog)
             </a>
             into the classpath, which might tip the total method count over 64k.
            </p>
            <p>
             That would force the use of proguard or
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/tools/building/multidex.html">
              multidex
             </a>
             even for debug builds. For one of my projects i had the following build times
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              multidex build (with supportlibrary) ~40sec
             </li>
             <li>
              proguard build ~20sec
             </li>
             <li>
              build when method limit &lt; 64k ~5sec
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             If developing on sdk 21+, it would possible to optimize multidex builds as stated
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/tools/building/multidex.html#dev-build">
              in the android documentation
             </a>
            </p>
            <pre><code>android {
    productFlavors {
        // Define separate dev and prod product flavors.
        dev {
            // dev utilizes minSDKVersion = 21 to allow the Android gradle plugin
            // to pre-dex each module and produce an APK that can be tested on
            // Android Lollipop without time consuming dex merging processes.
            minSdkVersion 21
        }
        prod {
            // The actual minSdkVersion for the application.
            minSdkVersion 14
        }
    }
    ...
}
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <a name="31633775">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="31633775" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16775197" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="16" id="answer-31633775" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="31633775">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="16" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             16
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/31633775/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The accepted answer is for older versions of android studio and most of them works still now. Updating android studio made it a little bit faster. Don't bother to specify heap size as it'll increase automatically with the increase of Xms and Xmx. Here's some modification with the VMoptions
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               In bin folder there's a studio.vmoptions file to set the environment configuration. In my case this is studio64.vmoptions
Add the following lines if they're not added already and save the file. In my case I've 8GB RAM.
              </p>
              <pre><code>-Xms4096m
-Xmx4096m
-XX:MaxPermSize=2048m
-XX:+CMSClassUnloadingEnabled
-XX:+CMSPermGenSweepingEnabled 
-XX:+HeapDumpOnOutOfMemoryError
-Dfile.encoding=utf-8`
</code></pre>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Start android studio. Go to File-&gt; Settings-&gt; Build, Execution, Deployment-&gt; Compiler
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Check compile independent modules in parallel
               </li>
               <li>
                In command-line Options write: --offline
               </li>
               <li>
                Check Make project automatically
               </li>
               <li>
                Check configure on demand
               </li>
              </ul>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             In case of using mac, at first I couldn't find the vmoptions. Anyway, here's a
             <a href="http://lifeofcoding.com/2015/01/19/How-to-increase-Android-studio-memory-limit-in-Mac/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              nice article about how we can change the vmoptions in MAC OSX
             </a>
             . Quoting from this article here.
            </p>
            <p>
             Open your terminal and put this command to open the vmoptions in MAC OSX:
            </p>
            <pre><code>open -e /Applications/Android\ Studio.app/Contents/bin/studio.vmoptions
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="22349752">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/22349752/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

            </a>

          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Just create a file named gradle.properties in the following directory:
            </p>
            <pre><code>/home/&lt;username&gt;/.gradle/ (Linux)
/Users/&lt;username&gt;/.gradle/ (Mac)
C:\Users\&lt;username&gt;\.gradle (Windows)
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Add this line to the file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>org.gradle.daemon=true
</code></pre>
            <p>
             For me the speed is now equal to Eclipse.
            </p>
            <p>
             Source:
             <a href="https://www.timroes.de/2013/09/12/speed-up-gradle/" rel="noreferrer">
              https://www.timroes.de/2013/09/12/speed-up-gradle/
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

            <p>
             You could make the process faster, if you use gradle from command line. There is a lot of optimization to do for the IDE developers. But it is just an early version.
            </p>
            <p>
             For more information read
             <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/110774282522099816721/posts/e9PG6vSN5w3" rel="noreferrer">
              this discussion
             </a>
             on g+ with some of the devs.

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If anyone is working a project which is synced via Subversion and this still happening, I think this can slow the process of workflow in Android Studio. For example if it work very slow while: scrolling in a class,xml etc, while my app is still running on my device.
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Go to Version Control at Preferences, and set from Subversion to None.
              <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/BpC9N.png" rel="noreferrer">
               <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/BpC9N.png"/>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="39654414">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <h1>
             <strong>
              Update After Android Studio 2.3
             </strong>
            </h1>
            <p>
             All answers are great, and I encourage to use those methods with this one to improve build speed.
            </p>
            <p>
             After release of android 2.2 on September 2016, Android released
             <em>
              experimental
             </em>
             build cache feature to speed up
             <code>
              gradle
             </code>
             build performance, which is now official from Android Studio 2.3 Canary.
             <a href="http://tools.android.com/tech-docs/build-cache" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              (Official Release note)
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             It introduces a new build cache feature, which is enable by default, can speed up build times (including full builds, incremental builds, and instant run) by storing and reusing files/directories that were created in previous builds of the same or different Android project.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              How to use:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Add following line in your
             <code>
              gradle.properties
             </code>
             file
            </p>
            <pre><code>android.enableBuildCache = true
# Set to true or false to enable or disable the build cache. If this parameter is not set, the build cache is enable by default.
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Clean the cache:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <p>
               There is a new Gradle task called
               <code>
                cleanBuildCache
               </code>
               for you to more easily clean the build cache. You can use it by typing the following in your terminal:
              </p>
              <p>
               <code>
                ./gradlew cleanBuildCache
               </code>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               OR You can clean the cache for Android studio 2.2 by deleting all the files store at location
              </p>
              <p>
               <code>
                C:\Users\&lt;username&gt;\.android\build-cache
               </code>
              </p>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>

            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35618854/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             After change this settings my compile duration 10 minutes changed to ~10 secs.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 1:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              Settings(ctrl+Alt+S) -&gt;
             </p>
             <p>
              Build,Execution,Deployment -&gt;
             </p>
             <p>
              Compiler -&gt;
             </p>
             <p>
              type "
              <code>
               --offline
              </code>
              " in command-line Options box.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 2:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              check the “Compile independent modules in parallel” checkbox.
             </p>
             <p>
              &amp; click Apply -&gt; OK
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/gjRRV.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/gjRRV.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Reference -
             <a href="https://www.sundoginteractive.com/blog/speed-up-gradle-in-android-studio" rel="noreferrer">
              https://www.sundoginteractive.com/blog/speed-up-gradle-in-android-studio
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Disadvantage:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             You will not be able to pull down the latest versions of the dependencies identified in your build.gradle file. It runs faster because it uses a cached snapshot of those imported libraries.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Important Note
             </strong>
             : When you deploy the application remove this settings &amp; build with latest versions of dependencies.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

             Solved mine with
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <code>
               File -&gt; Settings -&gt; Build, Execution, Deployment -&gt; Build Tools -&gt;
              </code>
              <code>
               Gradle -&gt; Offline work
              </code>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Gradle builds went from 8 minutes to 3 seconds.
            </p>

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="41080622" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16775197" data-position-on-page="14" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-41080622" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="41080622">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/41080622/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Here's what helped this beginning Android programmer (former professional programmer, years ago) in speeding up Android Studio 2.2. I know this is a rehash, but, just
             <strong>
              summarizing
             </strong>
             in one place.
            </p>
            <p>
             Initial builds can still be brutally slow, but restarts of running apps are now usually very tolerable. I'm using a sub-optimal PC: AMD Quad-Core A8-7410 CPU, 8MB RAM, non-SSD HD, Win 10. (And, this is my first Stack Overflow posting.... ;)
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              IN SETTINGS -&gt; GRADLE:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             yes for "Offline work"  (this is perhaps the most import setting).
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              IN SETTINGS -&gt; COMPILER:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             yes for "Compile independent modules in parallel"  (not sure if this does in fact help utilize multicore CPUs).
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              IN GRADLE SCRIPTS
             </strong>
             , "build.gradle (Module: app)":
            </p>
            <pre><code>defaultConfig {
    ...
   // keep min high so that restarted apps can be hotswapped...obviously, this is hugely faster.
   minSdkVersion 14
   ...
    // enabling multidex support...does make big difference for me.
    multiDexEnabled true
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              ALSO IN GRADLE SCRIPTS
             </strong>
             , "gradle.properties (Project Properties)":
            </p>
            <p>
             org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx3048m -XX:MaxPermSize=512m -XX:+HeapDumpOnOutOfMemoryError -Dfile.encoding=UTF-8
            </p>
            <p>
             org.gradle.parallel=true
org.gradle.daemon=true
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Additionally
             </strong>
             , testing on a physical device instead of the emulator is working well for me; a small tablet that stands up is convenient.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Just another performance imporvement tip:
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Android Studio 3.0
             </strong>
             includes new DEX compiler called D8.
            </p>
            <p>
             "The dex compiler mostly works under the hood in your day-to-day app development, but it directly impacts your app's build time, .dex file size, and runtime performance."
            </p>
            <p>
             "And when comparing the new D8 compiler with the current DX compiler, D8 compiles faster and outputs smaller .dex files, while having the same or better app runtime performance."
            </p>
            <p>
             D8 is optional - do use it we have to put to project's gradle.properties
            </p>
            <pre><code>android.enableD8=true
</code></pre>
            <p>
             More informations:
             <a href="https://android-developers.googleblog.com/2017/08/next-generation-dex-compiler-now-in.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://android-developers.googleblog.com/2017/08/next-generation-dex-compiler-now-in.html
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             PS. It impove my build time by about 30%.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="38187391">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/38187391/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This setup goes really fast for me 
(about 2 seconds the build)
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              build.gradle
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>android {

    dexOptions {
        incremental true
        preDexLibraries = false
        jumboMode = false
        maxProcessCount 4
        javaMaxHeapSize "6g"
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              gradle.properties
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>org.gradle.daemon=true
org.gradle.parallel=true
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx8192M
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              my PC:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              CPU  Intel(R) Pentium(R) CPU G2030 @ 3.00GHz, 3000 Mhz, 2 procesadores
principales, 2 procesadores lógicos
             </li>
             <li>
              x64
             </li>
             <li>
              Microsoft Windows 7 Professional
             </li>
             <li>
              (RAM) 16,0 GB
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <strong>
              project files
             </strong>
             <br/>
             - All located in local HD
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="41054122" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16775197" data-position-on-page="17" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-41054122" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="41054122">

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Please follow the following steps.
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Enable offline mode :  Please check below print screen.
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/RF9uG.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                https://i.stack.imgur.com/RF9uG.png
               </a>
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Enable Instant Run : Please check below print screen.
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/mvHKJ.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                https://i.stack.imgur.com/mvHKJ.png
               </a>
              </p>
              <p>
               If you want to learn more about instant run please visit android developer site.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>

            <p>
             You could try opening the gradle menu on the right side of studio, and assemble only the modules you have changed, then run the install command. When you press run it assembles everything regardless of any changes you you may have made to the code it is assembling
            </p>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="21817916" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16775197" data-position-on-page="19" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-21817916" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="21817916">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/21817916/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I'm far from being an expert on Gradle but my environment had the following line in .gradle/init.gradle
            </p>
            <pre><code>gradle.projectsLoaded {
    rootProject.allprojects {
        repositories {
            mavenRepo name: 'libs-repo', url: 'http://guest-vm/artifactory/repo'
        }
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Yet I have no idea why that line was there, but I try changing to
            </p>
            <pre><code>gradle.projectsLoaded {
    rootProject.allprojects {
        repositories {
            mavenCentral()
        }
    }
} 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             and now I finally can work without swearing to Android Studio &amp; Gradle buildind scheme.
            </p>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="49641812" data-comment-owner-id="1599472" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-49641812">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 artifactory in your case was probably used as a library cache. You contact the artifactory server which look if it have the library. If yes it return it to you otherwise it goes and fetch it from mavencentral and then return to you.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1599472/fabio-marcolini" title="2,237 reputation">
                  Fabio Marcolini
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2015-06-12 06:13:35Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Jun 12, 2015 at 6:13
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 1 time">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">
                  <path d="m11.1 1.71 1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0ZM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88Z">
                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In our specific case, the problem was due to having the
             <strong>
              retrolambda
             </strong>
             plugin, which forced all projects and subprojects to recompile everytime we tried to launch our application, even if no code had been altered in our core modules.
            </p>
            <p>
             Removing
             <strong>
              retrolamba
             </strong>
             fixed it for us. Hope it helps someone.
            </p>
           </div>

             I had the same problem. What i had done is just permanently disable the antivirus (Mine was Avast Security 2015). Just after  disabling the antivirus , thing gone well.   the gradle  finished successfully. 
From now within seconds the gradle is finishing ( Only taking 5-10 secs).

           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="35605922">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Hi I know this is very very late answer but maybe help someone
             <br/>
             in my case I was using
            </p>
            <pre><code>compile 'com.android.support:support-v4:23.1.1'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             in my app Gradle dependency
             <br/>
             but in one of my libraries it was
            </p>
            <pre><code> compile 'com.android.support:support-v4:23.0.1'
</code></pre>
            <p>
             after change all to latest version my problem solved.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Following the steps will make it 10 times faster and reduce build time 90%
            </p>
            <p>
             First create a file named gradle.properties in the following directory:
            </p>
            <pre><code>/home/&lt;username&gt;/.gradle/ (Linux)
/Users/&lt;username&gt;/.gradle/ (Mac)
C:\Users\&lt;username&gt;\.gradle (Windows)
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Add this line to the file:
            </p>
            <pre><code>org.gradle.daemon=true
org.gradle.parallel=true
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And check this options in Android Studio
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1y4t4.png" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1y4t4.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

            <p>
             USE this
sudo dpkg --add-architecture i386
sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get install libncurses5:i386 libstdc++6:i386 zlib1g:i386
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/30111443/android-studio-fails-to-build-new-project-timed-out-while-wating-for-slave-aapt/31095817#31095817">

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/41501650/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             A
             <strong>
              trivial
             </strong>
             change (to a resoruce xml) still took
             <strong>
              10 minutes
             </strong>
             .
As
             <strong>
              @rivare
             </strong>
             says in his answer, a command line build is mutch faster (took this down to
             <strong>
              15
             </strong>
             <strong>
              seconds
             </strong>
             ).
             <br/>
             Here are some steps to at least make a trivial build fast from the command line for Windows.
             <br/>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               <strong>
                Go
               </strong>
               to your projects root (where the gradlew.bat is):
              </p>
              <p>
               cd c:\android\MaskActivity
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               execute the
               <strong>
                build
               </strong>
               :
              </p>
              <p>
               gradlew assembleDebug
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               <strong>
                uninstall
               </strong>
               the apk from the phone directly (drag it to uninstall).
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               When the build is finished,
               <strong>
                kill
               </strong>
               the BIG java process using Windows
Task Manager.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             OR if you have unix tools on your Windows machine:
            </p>
            <pre><code>ps
</code></pre>
            <p>
             "pid" 's are shown:
            </p>
            <pre><code>kill -9 &lt;pid&gt;
</code></pre>
            <ol start="5">
             <li>
              <p>
               Now
               <strong>
                install
               </strong>
               your apk:
              </p>
              <p>
               adb -d install C:\Android\MaskActivity\app\build\outputs\apk\app-debug.apk
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             According to the
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/studio/build/optimize-your-build.html#dex_options" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              android documentation
             </a>
             , add this in the gradle file of app module.
            </p>
            <pre><code>android {
    ...
    dexOptions {
    preDexLibraries true
    maxProcessCount 8
    }
}
</code></pre>

        <a name="46465885">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="46465885" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="16775197" data-position-on-page="27" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-46465885" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="46465885">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/46465885/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              To run Android envirorment on low configuration machine.
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Close the uncessesory web tabs in browser
             </li>
             <li>
              For Antivirus users, exclude the build folder which is auto generated
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Android studio have 1.2 Gb default heap can decrease to 512 MB
Help &gt; Edit custom VM options
studio.vmoptions
-Xmx512m
Layouts performace will be speed up
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               For Gradle one of the core component in Android studio Mkae sure
like right now 3.0beta is latest one
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Below tips can affect the code quality so please use with cautions:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Studio contain Power safe Mode when turned on it will close background operations that lint , code complelitions and so on.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               You can run manually lintcheck when needed ./gradlew lint
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Most of are using Android emulators on average it consume 2 GB RAM so if possible use actual Android device these will reduce your resource load on your computer. Alternatively you can reduce the RAM of the emulator and it will automatically reduce the virtual memory consumption on your computer. you can find this in virtual device configuration and advance setting.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Gradle offline mode is a feature for bandwidth limited users to disable the downloading of build dependencies. It will reduce the background operation that will help to increase the performance of Android studio.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Android studio offers an optimization to compile multiple modules in parallel. On low RAM machines this feature will likely have a negative impact on the performance. You can disable it in the compiler settings dialog.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I was fed up with the slow build of android on my local machine. The way I solved this was spinning up a high-end machine on AWS and rsyncing the code from my local to the machine and compiling it over there.
            </p>
            <p>
             I saw an immediate increase in the performance and my local system was saved from CPU hog. Check out this tool I created to help the developers speed up their terminal
             <a href="https://stormyapp.com" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://stormyapp.com
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
